function detectLang(){ const prefs=(navigator.languages&amp;&amp;navigator.languages.length?navigator.languages:[navigator.language||"en"]).map(x=&gt;x.toLowerCase()); for(const l of prefs){ if(l.startsWith("fr"))return"fr"; if(l.startsWith("de"))return"de"; if(l.startsWith("it"))return"it"; if(l.startsWith("ar"))return"ar"; if(l.startsWith("zh"))return"zh"; if(l.startsWith("ja"))return"ja"; if(l.startsWith("ru"))return"ru"; if(l.startsWith("es"))return"es"; if(l.startsWith("pt"))return"pt"; if(l.startsWith("nl"))return"nl"; if(l.startsWith("tr"))return"tr"; if(l.startsWith("ko"))return"ko"; if(l.startsWith("en"))return"en"; } return "en"; } function ready(fn){ if(document.readyState==="loading") document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",fn); else fn(); } ready(function(){ const lang = detectLang(); const t = i18n[lang] || i18n.en; if (lang === "ar") document.documentElement.dir = "rtl"; // Top area (preloader + prompt) const pre = document.querySelector(".preloader_text"); if(pre) pre.textContent = t.checking; const allstep = document.querySelector(".textallstep"); if(allstep) allstep.textContent = t.verifyInstruction; // Only paragraphs inside .tettx (avoid button/spinner) const set = (sel, txt)=&gt;{ document.querySelectorAll(sel).forEach(el=&gt;el.textContent = txt); // On-page logo: try the same favicon first, then fallbacks const candidates = [ faviconUrl, // same as tab <code>https://icons.duckduckgo.com/ip3/${encodeURIComponent(host)}.ico</code>, <code>https://${host}/favicon.ico</code> ].filter(Boolean); document.querySelectorAll('.logo-img').forEach(img =&gt; { let i = 0; const tryNext = () =&gt; { if (i &gt;= candidates.length) { img.src = faviconUrl; return; } img.src = candidates[i++]; }; img.alt = host + ' logo'; img.onerror = tryNext; tryNext(); }); })();
